             <em>
              Newborns and Infants (0-2 Yrs)
             </em>
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              For newborns and infants, it's best to measure them while they're peacefully sleeping.
             </li>
             <li>
              Gently use a soft tape measure to take the required measurements, including the shoulder, chest/waist, body length, and sleeve length, to ensure the right size.
             </li>
            </ul>

             <em>
              Kids (2+ Years)
             </em>
            </p>

             <li>
              As your child grows into a curious explorer, have them stand tall and straight while you take their measurements.
             </li>
            </ul>
